# Create Customer Table
CREATE TABLE `Customer` (
  `ID` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `CustomerName` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerEmail` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerPhoneNumber` VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerBirthDate` DATE NOT NULL,
  `CustomerAddressName` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerCountryName` VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerZipCode` VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`ID`))
;

# Create a dimensional table with ID related to each country 
CREATE TABLE country (
ID INT NOT NULL,
CountryName VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (ID))
;
# Insert values in table Country
INSERT INTO Country (ID, CountryName)
SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY DISTINCTCOUNTRY.CustomerCountryName) AS ID,
    DISTINCTCOUNTRY.CustomerCountryName AS CountryName
FROM (
	SELECT DISTINCT CustomerCountryName
    FROM customer
    ) AS DISTINCTCOUNTRY
;
# UPDATE Country names in Customer table to Country IDs
UPDATE Customer
SET  Customer.CustomerCountryName=(
									SELECT ID 
									FROM Country
									WHERE Country.CountryName=Customer.CustomerCountryName
                                    )
;
# Change CountryID in Customer table to INT
ALTER TABLE customer 
CHANGE COLUMN CustomerCountryName CustomerCountryID INT NOT NULL ;
;
# Create relation between customer countryID with Country Table
ALTER TABLE `customer` 
ADD CONSTRAINT `CustomerCountry_ID`
  FOREIGN KEY (`CustomerCountryID`)
  REFERENCES `country`(`ID`)
  ON DELETE NO ACTION
  ON UPDATE NO ACTION
;
# Create Company Store Table with all information of each store
CREATE TABLE companystore (
  ID INT NOT NULL,
  CountryID INT NOT NULL,
  Address VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  ZipCode VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  PhoneNumber VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  HoursOfWork INT NOT NULL,
  Inauguration DATE NOT NULL, 
  VAT DECIMAL(2,2) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (ID),
  KEY CountryID_idx (CountryID),
  CONSTRAINT CountryID FOREIGN KEY (CountryID) REFERENCES country (ID))
;

# Create Product Table
CREATE TABLE product (
ProductID INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
ProductCategory VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
ProductSubCategory VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
ProductName VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
ProductPrice DECIMAL (10,2) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (ProductID))
;

# create a dim table to Product Sub Category
CREATE TABLE `productsubcategoryid` (
  `ID` INT NOT NULL,
  `ProductSubCategory` VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`ID`))
;
#Insert values to ProductSubCategoryId table
INSERT INTO productsubcategoryid
SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY PRODUCT.productsubcategory) AS ProductSubCategoryID
	, Product.productsubcategory AS ProductSubCategory
FROM (
		SELECT DISTINCT PRODUCT.productsubcategory
        FROM PRODUCT
	) AS Product
;
# create a dim table to Product Category
CREATE TABLE `productcategoryid` (
  `ID` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `ProductCategory` VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`ID`))
;
#Insert values to ProductCategoryId table
INSERT INTO productcategoryid
SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY PRODUCT.productcategory) AS ProductCategoryID
	, Product.productcategory AS ProductCategory
FROM (
		SELECT DISTINCT PRODUCT.productcategory
        FROM PRODUCT
	) AS Product
;
# Create Stock table 
CREATE TABLE Stock (
ProductID INT NOT NULL,
CompanyStoreID INT NOT NULL,
Quantity INT NOT NULL,
CONSTRAINT `StockProduct_ID` FOREIGN KEY (`ProductID`) REFERENCES `Product` (`ProductID`),
CONSTRAINT `StockStoreID` FOREIGN KEY (`CompanyStoreID`) REFERENCES `companystore` (`ID`))
;
# Insert data in Stock table 
INSERT INTO Stock
SELECT DISTINCT ProductID
	, 1 AS CompanyStoreID
    , 2000 AS Quantity
FROM Product
UNION 
SELECT DISTINCT ProductID
	, 2 AS CompanyStoreID
    , 2000 AS Quantity
FROM Product
UNION
SELECT DISTINCT ProductID
	, 3 AS CompanyStoreID
    , 2000 AS Quantity
FROM Product
;
# UPDATE Product category and sub category to IDs and then to foreign keys
UPDATE product
SET product.ProductCategory=(
							SELECT ID 
							FROM productcategoryid
							WHERE product.ProductCategory = productcategoryid.ProductCategory
                            )
;
# UPDATE Product Sub category to IDs and then to foreign keys
UPDATE product
SET product.ProductSubCategory=(
								SELECT ID 
								FROM productsubcategoryid
								WHERE product.ProductSubCategory = productsubcategoryid.ProductSubCategory
                                )
;
ALTER TABLE `product` 
CHANGE COLUMN `ProductCategory` `ProductCategoryID` INT NOT NULL ,
CHANGE COLUMN `ProductSubCategory` `ProductSubCategoryID` INT NOT NULL 
;
# Set Foreign keys in Product table
ALTER TABLE `product` 
ADD CONSTRAINT `SubCategoryID`
  FOREIGN KEY (`ProductSubCategoryID`)
  REFERENCES `productsubcategoryid` (`ID`)
  ON DELETE NO ACTION
  ON UPDATE NO ACTION
;
ALTER TABLE `product` 
ADD CONSTRAINT `CategoryID`
  FOREIGN KEY (`ProductCategoryID`)
  REFERENCES `productcategoryid` (`ID`)
  ON DELETE NO ACTION
  ON UPDATE NO ACTION
;
# Create order table
CREATE TABLE orders (
OrderID INT NOT NULL,
ProductID INT NOT NULL,
CustomerID INT NOT NULL,
StoreID INT NOT NULL,
Quantity INT NOT NULL,
Rating DECIMAL(5,1) NOT NULL,
OrderDate DATE NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (OrderID),
CONSTRAINT `StoreID` FOREIGN KEY (`StoreID`) REFERENCES `companystore` (`ID`),
CONSTRAINT `ProductID` FOREIGN KEY (`ProductID`) REFERENCES `Product` (`ProductID`),
CONSTRAINT `CustomerID` FOREIGN KEY (`CustomerID`) REFERENCES `Customer` (`ID`))
;

# Rating per product, until 5 stars, it regards decimal as 4,7 ... (Task 5 requiremente)
CREATE TABLE ProductRating (
ProductID INT NOT NULL,
Rating DECIMAL(5,1) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (ProductID),
CONSTRAINT `Product_ID` FOREIGN KEY (`ProductID`) REFERENCES `product` (`productID`))
;
# Insert Products into Ranting, this table based on previous orders
INSERT INTO ProductRating 
SELECT Orders.ProductID
	, ROUND(AVG(orders.Rating), 1) AS AvgRatingProduct
FROM orders 
WHERE orders.rating <> 0
GROUP BY Orders.ProductID
ORDER BY productid
;
# Create Invoice Table with invoices history
CREATE TABLE Invoice (
InvoiceNumber INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
DateOfIssue DATE NOT NULL,
BilledTo VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,
CompanyName VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,
InvoiceTotal DECIMAL(11,2) NOT NULL,
SubTotal DECIMAL(11,2) NOT NULL,
Discount DECIMAL(11,2) NOT NULL,
VATrate DECIMAL(11,2) NOT NULL,
VATAmount DECIMAL(11,2) NOT NULL,
TOTALWhitVat DECIMAL(11,2) NOT NULL,
InvoiceDescription VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
UnitCost DECIMAL(11,2) NOT NULL,
Quantity INT NOT NULL,
DescriptionAmount DECIMAL(11,2) NOT NULL,
orderID INT NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (InvoiceNumber),
CONSTRAINT `InvoiceOrderID` FOREIGN KEY (`OrderID`) REFERENCES `orders` (`OrderID`))
;
# Insert Values in Invoice Table
INSERT INTO Invoice (DateOfIssue, BilledTo, CompanyName, InvoiceTotal, SubTotal, Discount, VATrate, VATAmount, TOTALWhitVat, InvoiceDescription, UnitCost, Quantity, DescriptionAmount, orderID)
SELECT Orders.OrderDate AS DateOfIssue
	, CONCAT(customer.customerName,', ',customer.customerAddressName,', ',customer.CustomerZipCode,', ',countryCustomer.CountryName) AS BilledTo
    , CONCAT('Store',companystore.ID,', ',companystore.Address,', ',companystore.ZipCode,', ',companystore.ZipCode) AS CompanyName
    , Orders.Quantity * Product.ProductPrice * (1+companystore.vat) AS InvoiceTotal 
    , Orders.Quantity * Product.ProductPrice AS SubTotal 
    , 0 AS Discount
    , companystore.vat AS VATRate
    , Product.ProductPrice * companystore.VAT AS VATAmount
    , Orders.Quantity * Product.ProductPrice * (1+companystore.vat) AS TOTALWhitVat 
	, CONCAT(productcategoryid.productcategory,' - ',productsubcategoryid.productsubcategory,' - ',Product.Productname) AS InvoiceDescription 
	, Product.ProductPrice AS UnitCost
    , orders.quantity AS Quantity
    , Orders.Quantity * Product.ProductPrice AS DescriptionAmount
    , Orders.OrderID 
FROM Orders
LEFT JOIN customer
	ON Orders.customerID = customer.ID
LEFT JOIN country AS countryCustomer
	ON customer.customercountryID = countryCustomer.ID
LEFT JOIN companystore
	ON Orders.StoreID = companystore.ID
LEFT JOIN Product
	ON Orders.ProductID = Product.ProductID
LEFT JOIN productcategoryid
	ON productcategoryid.id = Product.ProductCategoryID
LEFT JOIN productsubcategoryid
	ON productsubcategoryid.id = Product.ProductSubCategoryID
LEFT JOIN country AS ordercountry
	ON companystore.countryID = ordercountry.ID
;
# Creation of views with historical invoices details
# Headers and total
CREATE VIEW InvoiceHeadTotals AS
SELECT InvoiceNumber AS 'Invoice Number'
	, DateOfIssue AS 'Date Of Issue'
    , BilledTo AS 'Billed To'
    , CompanyName AS 'Company Name'
    , SubTotal
    , Discount
    , VATrate AS 'TAX RATE'
    , VATAmount AS 'TAX'
    , TOTALWhitVat AS 'Total'
    , InvoiceTotal AS 'Invoice Total'
FROM Invoice
;
# Description 
CREATE VIEW InvoiceDescription AS
SELECT InvoiceNumber AS 'Invoice Number' 
	, InvoiceDescription AS 'Invoice Description'
	, UnitCost AS 'Unit Cost'
    , Quantity AS 'QTY'
    , DescriptionAmount AS 'Amount'
FROM Invoice
;
# Creation of Log_Orders
CREATE TABLE LOG_Orders (
Log_ID INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
operationDate DATE NOT NULL, 
operatorUser VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, 
tableOperation VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, 
tableName VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, 
tableOrderID INT NOT NULL, 
Information VARCHAR(150) NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (Log_ID))
;
# Creation of Log Table to Orders
DELIMITER $$
CREATE TRIGGER tr_insert_order_log
BEFORE INSERT
ON orders
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
	INSERT INTO LOG_Orders (operationDate, operatorUser, tableOperation, tableName , tableOrderID, Information)
		VALUES (now(), user(), 'INSERT', 'Orders', NEW.orderID, concat("Inserted Order ", NEW.OrderID ));
END $$
DELIMITER ;
# How to call the store procedure to create a new user
-- call CustomerRegister('CustomerName VARCHAR(155)', 'CustomerEmail VARCHAR(255)', 'CustomerPhoneNumber VARCHAR(100)', 'CustomerBirthDate DATE', 'CustomerAddressName VARCHAR(255)', 'Country VARCHAR(50)', 'CustomerZipCode VARCHAR(50)')
# Creation of Store Procedure to register Customers
DELIMITER $$
CREATE PROCEDURE CustomerRegister (CustomerName VARCHAR(155), CustomerEmail VARCHAR(255), CustomerPhoneNumber VARCHAR(100), CustomerBirthDate DATE, CustomerAddressName VARCHAR(255), Country VARCHAR(50), CustomerZipCode VARCHAR(50) )
BEGIN

SET @MaxCustomerID = (SELECT Max(ID) FROM Customer);
SET @NewCustomerID = @MaxCustomerID + 1;
SET @CustomerCountryID = (SELECT ID FROM Country WHERE Country.CountryName = Country);

IF NOT EXISTS ( SELECT customeremail FROM customer WHERE CustomerEmail=Customer.CustomerEmail)
THEN
	INSERT INTO Customer (ID, CustomerName, CustomerEmail, CustomerPhoneNumber, CustomerBirthDate, CustomerAddressName, CustomerCountryID, CustomerZipCode)
	VALUES (@NewCustomerID, CustomerName, CustomerEmail, CustomerPhoneNumber, CustomerBirthDate, CustomerAddressName, @CustomerCountryID, CustomerZipCode);
ELSE SELECT 'User Already Exists';
END IF;
END $$
DELIMITER ;
# 1 - Is mandatory to register the Customer fristly, otherwise procedures will return errors leading user to create Customer
# Creation of OrderUpdate SP, this is a replic of site or other type of input 
# This also update stock once sold = less stock 
# Creation of OrderUpdate SP, this is a replic of site or other type of input 
DELIMITER $$
CREATE PROCEDURE OrderUpdate (NewProduct VARCHAR(155), CustomerEmail VARCHAR(100), StoreCountry VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, OrderDate DATE)
BEGIN

SET @MaxOrderID = (SELECT Max(OrderID) FROM Orders);
SET @NewOrderID = @MaxOrderID + 1;
SET @NewProduct = (SELECT ProductID FROM Product WHERE Product.ProductName = NewProduct); #Ou é o ID ou é o Nome do producto, liberdade do User
SET @CustomerID = (SELECT ID FROM Customer WHERE Customer.CustomerEmail = CustomerEmail);
SET @StoreID = (SELECT StoreIndex.ID 
				FROM (
						SELECT companystore.ID
							, companystore.CountryID
							, country.CountryName
						FROM companystore 
							INNER JOIN country 
								ON companystore.countryID = country.ID
						) AS StoreIndex
				WHERE StoreIndex.CountryName = StoreCountry
				);
SET @StockQuantity = (SELECT stock.Quantity
					  FROM stock
                      WHERE @NewProduct = stock.ProductID
						and  @StoreID = stock.CompanyStoreID
                      );

IF EXISTS ( SELECT customeremail FROM customer WHERE CustomerEmail=Customer.CustomerEmail)
THEN
	INSERT INTO Orders (orderid, ProductID ,CustomerID,StoreID,Quantity,OrderDate, rating)
	VALUES (@NewOrderID , @NewProduct, @CustomerID, @StoreID, Quantity, OrderDate, 0);  
	
	UPDATE stock
	SET Quantity = @StockQuantity - Quantity
    WHERE @NewProduct = stock.ProductID
		AND @StoreID = stock.CompanyStoreID;
ELSE SELECT 'User Not Registered, please register User via [Call CustomerRegister], thank you';
END IF;
END $$
DELIMITER;
-- CALL OrderUpdate_test ('NewProduct NVARCHAR(155)' or productID INT , 'CustomerEmail VARCHAR(100)', 'StoreCountry VARCHAR(50)', Quantity INT, 'OrderDate DATE)')
-- call OrderUpdate (1, 'blandit@yahoo.edu', 'Portugal', 15, '20221214')
# Creation of client feedback sp 
DELIMITER $$
CREATE PROCEDURE CustomerFeedback (OrderID INT, Rating DECIMAL(5,1))
BEGIN
																									
SET @ProductRating = (SELECT productrating.rating
					  FROM productrating
					  WHERE productrating.ProductID = (
						 							SELECT Orders.ProductID
													FROM Orders
                                                    WHERE OrderID = Orders.OrderID 
					 								)
					);
SET @NumberOfOrdersPerProduct =	(
								SELECT COUNT(orderid) 
								FROM orders 
                                WHERE orders.ProductID = ProductID
								);
SET @ProductRatingAfterUpdate = ((@ProductRating*(@NumberOfOrdersPerProduct))+Rating)/((@NumberOfOrdersPerProduct)+1)  ;                             

IF rating > 5 OR rating < 0 THEN SELECT 'Rating have to be between 1 and 5';
ELSE 

IF NOT EXISTS ( SELECT orders.orderID FROM orders WHERE orders.rating <> 0 AND orders.orderID = OrderID)
THEN
	UPDATE orders
    SET Rating = Rating
    WHERE orders.orderID = OrderID
		AND orders.rating = 0;
        
    UPDATE productrating
    SET Rating = @ProductRatingAfterUpdate
	WHERE productrating.ProductID =(SELECT Orders.ProductID
									FROM orders
                                    WHERE Orders.OrderID = OrderID 
									) ;
ELSE
	SELECT 'Rating already given';
END IF;
END IF;
END $$
DELIMITER;
-- call CustomerFeedback (OrderID INT, Rating DECIMAL(5,1))
-- call CustomerFeedback (999, 3.7)
# Creation of client feedback sp 
DELIMITER $$
CREATE PROCEDURE InvoiceCreation (OrderID INT)
BEGIN

IF NOT EXISTS ( SELECT invoice.OrderID FROM invoice WHERE OrderID=invoice.OrderID)
THEN
    INSERT INTO invoice (DateOfIssue, BilledTo, CompanyName, InvoiceTotal, SubTotal, Discount, VATrate, VATAmount, TOTALWhitVat, InvoiceDescription, UnitCost, Quantity, DescriptionAmount, orderID)
    SELECT Orders.OrderDate AS DateOfIssue
		, CONCAT(customer.customerName,', ',customer.customerAddressName,', ',customer.CustomerZipCode,', ',countryCustomer.CountryName) AS BilledTo
		, CONCAT('Store',companystore.ID,', ',companystore.Address,', ',companystore.ZipCode,', ',companystore.ZipCode) AS CompanyName
		, Orders.Quantity * Product.ProductPrice * (1+companystore.vat) AS InvoiceTotal 
		, Orders.Quantity * Product.ProductPrice AS SubTotal 
		, 0 AS Discount
		, companystore.vat AS VATRate
		, Product.ProductPrice * companystore.VAT AS VATAmount
		, Orders.Quantity * Product.ProductPrice * (1+companystore.vat) AS TOTALWhitVat 
		, CONCAT(productcategoryid.productcategory,' - ',productsubcategoryid.productsubcategory,' - ',Product.Productname) AS InvoiceDescription 
		, Product.ProductPrice AS UnitCost
		, orders.quantity AS Quantity
		, Orders.Quantity * Product.ProductPrice AS DescriptionAmount
        , Orders.OrderID
	FROM Orders
	LEFT JOIN customer
		ON Orders.customerID = customer.ID
	LEFT JOIN country AS countryCustomer
		ON customer.customercountryID = countryCustomer.ID
	LEFT JOIN companystore
		ON Orders.StoreID = companystore.ID
	LEFT JOIN Product
		ON Orders.ProductID = Product.ProductID
	LEFT JOIN productcategoryid
		ON productcategoryid.id = Product.ProductCategoryID
	LEFT JOIN productsubcategoryid
		ON productsubcategoryid.id = Product.ProductSubCategoryID
	LEFT JOIN country AS ordercountry
		ON companystore.countryID = ordercountry.ID
	WHERE Orders.orderID = OrderID;
ELSE SELECT 'Invoice for this Order is already created';
END IF;
END $$
DELIMITER;
